# Weather Lens - Complete Regions List

**Total Regions: 3,616**

**Coastal Summary:**
- Total Coastal: 653
- 동해 (East Sea): 171
- 서해 (West Sea): 216
- 남해 (South Sea): 329

## Data Fields

- **Code**: Official region code
- **Emd**: Township/Neighborhood (읍면동)
- **Lat/Lon**: Geographic coordinates (WGS84)
- **NX/NY**: Korea Meteorological Administration grid coordinates
- **Elev**: Elevation in meters
- **Coastal**: EC=동해(East), WC=서해(West), SC=남해(South), - (not coastal)

---
